| // Check varargs and va_copy.
| static void
| test_varargs (const char *format, ...)
| {
|   va_list args;
|   va_start (args, format);
|   va_list args_copy;
|   va_copy (args_copy, args);
| 
|   const char *str;
|   int number;
|   float fnumber;
| 
|   while (*format)
|     {
|       switch (*format++)
| 	{
| 	case 's': // string
| 	  str = va_arg (args_copy, const char *);
| 	  break;
| 	case 'd': // int
| 	  number = va_arg (args_copy, int);
| 	  break;
| 	case 'f': // float
| 	  fnumber = va_arg (args_copy, double);
| 	  break;
| 	default:
| 	  break;
| 	}
|     }
|   va_end (args_copy);
|   va_end (args);
| }
